           <div class="u-posr c-home__section-head">
            <h2 class="b-h3 u-tac c-home__section-title">
             Our Connected Garden
            </h2>
           </div>
           <p class="lead">
            The Royal Botanic Garden Sydney and The Domain, Sydney are now Australia’s most extensive and digitally-connected spaces with 40 ‘smart-nodes’ providing
            <a href="/Stories/2018/Connect-with-the-Garden">
             free high-speed WiFi
            </a>
            throughout the Garden and Domain for visitors, plus we have a
            <a href="https://www.rbgsyd.nsw.gov.au/Stories/2018/Connect-with-the-Garden">
             brand-new app
            </a>
            <a href="/Stories/2018/Connect-with-the-Garden">
             .
            </a>
            <br/>
           </p>
